## <a name="windows-server-2012-extended-rights"></a><span data-ttu-id="68183-2476">Расширенные права Windows Server 2012</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="68183-2476">Windows Server 2012 Extended Rights</span></span>
